<p dir="auto"><strong>AI-powered command-line workflow tool for developers</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="#installation">Installation</a> • <a href="#quick-start">Quick Start</a> • <a href="#key-features">Features</a> • <a href="/QwenLM/qwen-code/blob/main/docs">Documentation</a> • <a href="/QwenLM/qwen-code/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md">Contributing</a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://qwenlm.github.io/qwen-code-docs/de/" rel="nofollow">Deutsch</a> |

<p dir="auto">Qwen Code is a powerful command-line AI workflow tool adapted from <a href="https://github.com/google-gemini/gemini-cli"><strong>Gemini CLI</strong></a>, specifically optimized for <a href="https://github.com/QwenLM/Qwen3-Coder">Qwen3-Coder</a> models. It enhances your development workflow with advanced code understanding, automated tasks, and intelligent assistance.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">💡 Free Options Available</h2><a id="user-content--free-options-available" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 💡 Free Options Available" href="#-free-options-available"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Get started with Qwen Code at no cost using any of these free options:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🔥 Qwen OAuth (Recommended)</h3><a id="user-content--qwen-oauth-recommended" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🔥 Qwen OAuth (Recommended)" href="#-qwen-oauth-recommended"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>2,000 requests per day</strong> with no token limits</li>
<li><strong>60 requests per minute</strong> rate limit</li>
<li>Simply run <code>qwen</code> and authenticate with your qwen.ai account</li>
<li>Automatic credential management and refresh</li>
<li>Use <code>/auth</code> command to switch to Qwen OAuth if you have initialized with OpenAI compatible mode</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">🌏 Regional Free Tiers</h3><a id="user-content--regional-free-tiers" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 🌏 Regional Free Tiers" href="#-regional-free-tiers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Mainland China</strong>: ModelScope offers <strong>2,000 free API calls per day</strong></li>
<li><strong>International</strong>: OpenRouter provides <strong>up to 1,000 free API calls per day</strong> worldwide</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For detailed setup instructions, see <a href="#authorization">Authorization</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning" dir="auto"><p class="markdown-alert-title" dir="auto"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p dir="auto"><strong>Token Usage Notice</strong>: Qwen Code may issue multiple API calls per cycle, resulting in higher token usage (similar to Claude Code). We're actively optimizing API efficiency.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Key Features</h2><a id="user-content-key-features" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Key Features" href="#key-features"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Code Understanding &amp; Editing</strong> - Query and edit large codebases beyond traditional context window limits</li>
<li><strong>Workflow Automation</strong> - Automate operational tasks like handling pull requests and complex rebases</li>
<li><strong>Enhanced Parser</strong> - Adapted parser specifically optimized for Qwen-Coder models</li>
<li><strong>Vision Model Support</strong> - Automatically detect images in your input and seamlessly switch to vision-capable models for multimodal analysis</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Installation</h2><a id="user-content-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Installation" href="#installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ensure you have <a href="https://nodejs.org/en/download" rel="nofollow">Node.js version 20</a> or higher installed.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -qL https://www.npmjs.com/install.sh | sh"><pre>curl -qL https://www.npmjs.com/install.sh <span class="pl-k">|</span> sh</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Install from npm</h3><a id="user-content-install-from-npm" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Install from npm" href="#install-from-npm"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quick Start" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Start Qwen Code
qwen

# Example commands
&gt; Explain this codebase structure
&gt; Help me refactor this function
&gt; Generate unit tests for this module"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Start Qwen Code</span>
qwen

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Example commands</span>
<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> Explain this codebase structure
<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> Help me refactor this function
<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> Generate unit tests <span class="pl-k">for</span> this module</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Session Management</h3><a id="user-content-session-management" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Session Management" href="#session-management"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Control your token usage with configurable session limits to optimize costs and performance.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Configure Session Token Limit</h4><a id="user-content-configure-session-token-limit" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Configure Session Token Limit" href="#configure-session-token-limit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Create or edit <code>.qwen/settings.json</code> in your home directory:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;sessionTokenLimit&quot;: 32000
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"sessionTokenLimit"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">32000</span>
}</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Session Commands</h4><a id="user-content-session-commands" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Session Commands" href="#session-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>/compress</code></strong> - Compress conversation history to continue within token limits</li>
<li><strong><code>/clear</code></strong> - Clear all conversation history and start fresh</li>
<li><strong><code>/stats</code></strong> - Check current token usage and limits</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">📝 <strong>Note</strong>: Session token limit applies to a single conversation, not cumulative API calls.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Vision Model Configuration</h3><a id="user-content-vision-model-configuration" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Vision Model Configuration" href="#vision-model-configuration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Qwen Code includes intelligent vision model auto-switching that detects images in your input and can automatically switch to vision-capable models for multimodal analysis. <strong>This feature is enabled by default</strong> - when you include images in your queries, you'll see a dialog asking how you'd like to handle the vision model switch.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Skip the Switch Dialog (Optional)</h4><a id="user-content-skip-the-switch-dialog-optional" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Skip the Switch Dialog (Optional)" href="#skip-the-switch-dialog-optional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">If you don't want to see the interactive dialog each time, configure the default behavior in your <code>.qwen/settings.json</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;experimental&quot;: {
    &quot;vlmSwitchMode&quot;: &quot;once&quot;
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"experimental"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"vlmSwitchMode"</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>once<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Available modes:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><code>"once"</code></strong> - Switch to vision model for this query only, then revert</li>
<li><strong><code>"session"</code></strong> - Switch to vision model for the entire session</li>
<li><strong><code>"persist"</code></strong> - Continue with current model (no switching)</li>
<li><strong>Not set</strong> - Show interactive dialog each time (default)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Command Line Override</h4><a id="user-content-command-line-override" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Command Line Override" href="#command-line-override"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">You can also set the behavior via command line:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Switch once per query
qwen --vlm-switch-mode once

# Switch for entire session
qwen --vlm-switch-mode session

# Never switch automatically
qwen --vlm-switch-mode persist"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Switch once per query</span>
qwen --vlm-switch-mode once

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Switch for entire session</span>
qwen --vlm-switch-mode session

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Never switch automatically</span>
qwen --vlm-switch-mode persist</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Disable Vision Models (Optional)</h4><a id="user-content-disable-vision-models-optional" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Disable Vision Models (Optional)" href="#disable-vision-models-optional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">To completely disable vision model support, add to your <code>.qwen/settings.json</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-json notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="{
  &quot;experimental&quot;: {
    &quot;visionModelPreview&quot;: false
  }
}"><pre>{
  <span class="pl-ent">"experimental"</span>: {
    <span class="pl-ent">"visionModelPreview"</span>: <span class="pl-c1">false</span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">💡 <strong>Tip</strong>: In YOLO mode (<code>--yolo</code>), vision switching happens automatically without prompts when images are detected.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Authorization</h3><a id="user-content-authorization" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Authorization" href="#authorization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Choose your preferred authentication method based on your needs:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Qwen OAuth (🚀 Recommended - Start in 30 seconds)</h4><a id="user-content-1-qwen-oauth--recommended---start-in-30-seconds" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. <p dir="auto">The easiest way to get started - completely free with generous quotas:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Just run this command and follow the browser authentication
qwen"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Just run this command and follow the browser authentication</span>
qwen</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>What happens:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li><strong>Instant Setup</strong>: CLI opens your browser automatically</li>
<li><strong>One-Click Login</strong>: Authenticate with your qwen.ai account</li>
<li><strong>Automatic Management</strong>: Credentials cached locally for future use</li>
<li><strong>No Configuration</strong>: Zero setup required - just start coding!</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Free Tier Benefits:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>✅ <strong>2,000 requests/day</strong> (no token counting needed)</li>
<li>✅ <strong>60 requests/minute</strong> rate limit</li>
<li>✅ <strong>Automatic credential refresh</strong></li>
<li>✅ <strong>Zero cost</strong> for individual users</li>
<li>ℹ️ <strong>Note</strong>: Model fallback may occur to maintain service quality</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. OpenAI-Compatible API</h4><a id="user-content-2-openai-compatible-api" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. <p dir="auto">Use API keys for OpenAI or other compatible providers:</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Configuration Methods:</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Environment Variables</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export OPENAI_API_KEY=&quot;your_api_key_here&quot;

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Project <code>.env</code> File</strong>
Create a <code>.env</code> file in your project root:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-dotenv notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="OPENAI_API_KEY=your_api_key_here

<span class="pl-v">OPENAI_MODEL</span><span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-s">your_model_choice</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ol>

<blockquote>

</ul>
</blockquote>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Session Commands</h3><a id="user-content-session-commands-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Session Commands" href="#session-commands-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>/help</code> - Display available commands</li>
<li><code>/clear</code> - Clear conversation history</li>
<li><code>/compress</code> - Compress history to save tokens</li>
<li><code>/stats</code> - Show current session information</li>
<li><code>/exit</code> or <code>/quit</code> - Exit Qwen Code</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Keyboard Shortcuts</h3><a id="user-content-keyboard-shortcuts" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Keyboard Shortcuts" href="#keyboard-shortcuts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>Ctrl+C</code> - Cancel current operation</li>
<li><code>Ctrl+D</code> - Exit (on empty line)</li>
<li><code>Up/Down</code> - Navigate command history</li>
</ul>
